We recall that the August Emperor establishes the Ultimate, having graciously served through three reigns; yet the Celestial Lord bestows his favor, and we shamefully remain unrefined in even a single virtue. Grounded in sincerity, we offer gratitude and confess our faults.

We, your servant, have early inherited the immortal lineage and repeatedly encountered flourishing fortune. Yet our transgressions accumulate like mountains, bringing forth the hardships of calamity and adversity; our afflictions deepen daily, making it difficult to preserve the harmony of our household. Our prayers of supplication have been twice prostrated, and the joy of peace has been twice reborn. May the talismanic decree align with the era of *Guanju*’s harmonious beginning, fulfilling the hope of bearing the peach of filial succession. With reverence, we repay our plain vows and extend deliverance to our forebears. Thus, we purify the offerings of fern and delicacies, presenting them to seek the scrutiny of the numinous mirror.

We pray that the Emperor’s oversight may shine forth, and Heaven’s hearing be most clear. May names be inscribed on the cinnabar tablets, turning inauspicious stars into auspicious omens; may jade talismans convey life, raising the sunken and stagnant from the depths of the unseen. May the model of the teaching be secure and prosperous, and the ancestral line rest in tranquility.

**Prayer Intention for the Ji-Si Offering**
Fortunate is the foundation of past blessings, having early inherited the rank of ancestral transmission; we bear the grace of the state and annually approach the sacred birthday of the Emperor. Yet we dread the great difficulty of audience and the perilous journey through wind and waves. Looking up, we beseech the offering and prayer, having already been bathed in the Mysterious Grace.

Yesterday, we petitioned for the removal of external burdens, relying truly on the protection of ultimate fulfillment. Suddenly afflicted by unexpected disturbances, we swiftly returned to safety. We have repeatedly prostrated in repentance and supplication, and together expressed gratitude for the support of creation.

We pray that the Emperor’s presence may reign above, and the numinous descent be most solemn. May he perceive the sincerity of human desires and forgive the accumulated stains of our transgressions. May the imperial realm flourish like a tripod, daily increasing the radiance of the teaching’s lineage; may the household’s blessings flow like spring, harmonizing with the revival of the ancestral way. May the gates and courtyards endure everlastingly, and peace and trust be universally upheld.

**Annual Prayer Intention of This Prefecture**
As the years complete their cycle, we have fortunately enjoyed peace through the four seasons; bearing the axis of the teaching, we strive to repay it with wholehearted sincerity. Moreover, though our faults and regrets have amassed, our vigilance and effort in cultivation have often been lacking. Whether disasters arise from earth and wood or afflictions from human affairs and illness, we have repeatedly presented our prostrations and supplications, and time and again been blessed with preservation.

Thus, we dutifully follow the custom of the year-end farewell and respectfully offer our bundles of gratitude. We, your servant, equally rely on the ancestral grace and look up to the favor of the state. We lack the warmth and care of morning and evening, mindful of the toils endured through cold and heat. Without the aid of repentance and release, how could we achieve the averting of faults?

We pray that our earnest sincerity may ascend, and health and peace be bestowed. May the sacred realm flourish like spring, and the perfect transformation of the teaching be exalted; may the foundation of blessings open in prosperity, and auspicious signs harmonize with the household. May all hoped-for blessings to come be granted by the great benevolence of creation. May longevity flourish like the mother’s orchid, and honor equal the twin blossoms of the hall.

**Prayer Intention for the Offering at the Round Terrace**
In the twenty-fifth year of Hongwu, incense was presented at Huagai Mountain. The Emperor’s command graciously descended to seek blessings for the Crown Prince; this humble servant, afflicted by illness, relied on his compassionate mother to pray for peace.

Moreover, my office is not one gained through deceit or usurpation, yet I harbor deep concerns about the perils of distant travel. I must examine myself with reverent fear, and seek divine favor through prayer and ritual. May the gods silently assist, and the covenant of this offering be fulfilled.

We humbly pray that Heaven bestow its boundless grace, and the stars shine with radiant splendor. May the blessings of our household grow ever more vast, and benevolence and longevity ascend together; may the foundation of the realm harmonize with enduring peace, and sagely plans expand without limit. May the mother’s orchid flourish in longevity, and the twin blossoms of the hall exude the fragrance of orchids.

**Intention for the Establishment of the Universal Salvation Offering**
I reflect that I early inherited the immortal lineage and have repeatedly received the Emperor’s favor. The merits of my ancestors weigh upon me, for I have failed to repay them as my original vow demanded; my words and deeds bear faults and transgressions, and I lament that not even a shred of goodness has been achieved. All is subject to impermanence, and the rise and fall of fortunes remain unfathomable. In addition to fulfilling my earnest prayers, I am ever mindful of the weight of my duties. I rely on this offering for deliverance, that all my transgressions may be absolved.

Truly, the great virtue delights in giving life, and responds with goodness though no words are spoken. We humbly pray that the Supreme One extend compassion from the northern pole, and the southern fire refine and temper. May the jade tally and golden writ swiftly open the clarity of the five portals; may the cinnabar realm and vermilion mound illuminate the nine depths like a torch. May grace extend to all creation, and blessings flow without end.

**Early Morning Prayer for Universal Salvation**
Heaven is high and Earth profound—how could one forget the grace of virtue? Days pass and months come, as swiftly as the exchange of past and present. I lay bare my sincerity and present my plea, exhausting my heart in this petition.

I reflect that I, though inheriting noble rank, am filled with shame when I examine myself and repent my faults. The debt of gratitude I owe, whether near or far, deepens my sorrow; the hope of deliverance for the departed in the unseen realm urges me to offer thanks without delay. Fearing that my transgressions remain unatoned, I must seek purification through repentance to dissolve them entirely. Thus, I purify this morning offering and fulfill my simple vows.

We humbly pray that the nine depths release the bound from their sins, and the five sufferings cease their bitterness. May the root of life be preserved, and all attain the fruit of carefree wandering; may they ascend to the realm of true joy, and restore the springtime of growth and renewal. May the radiance of the teaching spread, and the imperial favor bring auspicious harmony.

**Intention for the Universal Salvation Offering in the Jia-Shen Year**
I reflect that I have unworthily inherited the immortal lineage and enjoyed the favor of the sagely court. Yet my sins run deep, and I have failed to cleanse my faults. My prolonged illness has brought distress to my household, leaving no peace. I knock at the gates of sincerity, hoping the myriad spirits will respond. Humbly presenting this modest offering, I seek to repay the imperial grace.

We humbly pray that the sagely creation shine forth, and the Emperor’s heart hold us in favor. May past transgressions be dissolved, and misfortune swiftly give way to prosperity; may the dark realms be illuminated, and compassionate deliverance bring enlightenment. May the teaching’s influence be strengthened, and the household’s blessings flourish. May all within the realm of cultivation receive life and growth.

**Sincere Intention for the Establishment of the Offering at the Round Terrace**
The sun rises and the moon sets, bound by the mechanisms of time. Yin waxes as yang wanes, and I fear that misfortune will leave no peace. I look upward, hoping to reverse the course of adversity, and earnestly beseech the vast Heaven with my prayers. Though the rites have been delayed for four years, a single sincere offering may yet reach the divine. I repay my vows, though overdue, and await the fulfillment of grace.

We humbly pray that the imperial gaze shine brightly, and the Emperor’s benevolence spread boundlessly. May the teaching’s lineage endure like the mountains, and the five fortunes be fully bestowed; may the ancestral influence flourish like the rose, and a hundred auspicious signs gather. May disasters dissolve like melting ice, and joyous blessings converge in warmth.

**Address for the Raising of the Beam in the Three Clarities Hall**
We humbly observe that the Three Realms and the divine continents manifest in the formless above; the Five Sacred Peaks and blessed lands open upon the renowned mountains of the Dragon and Tiger. Though the world has shifted through the dust of kalpas, we now behold the resplendent renewal of this hall. The Emperor’s grace knows no bounds, and the Dao’s transformation is without limit.

We revere His Majesty the Emperor, whose greatness equals Heaven and Earth, and whose brilliance rivals the sun and moon. His governance establishes order across the ten thousand regions, and his cultural unity extends to the four seas. His magnificent achievements and virtuous power form the foundation of royal governance; his sagely descendants will further expand the eternal imperial plan. The Daoist gate holds him in highest esteem, and this splendid edifice is newly constructed.

We look up to the Three Clarities and Three Realms Heavenly Worthy, the Supreme Perfect of the Formless, the Primordial Lord. You preside as the original honored one of the three realms and govern the myriad heavens. From the mysterious origin, the beginning and completion took form; the pure and luminous coalesced, boundless and eternal. The purple writs and cinnabar texts expound the inner scriptures of the ten poles and nine skies; the golden codes and jade laws unfold the sacred chapters of the seven classics and eight wefts. Thus, the dragon scripts and phoenix seals are revealed, and the tiger guards and simurgh glues convene. The distant gaze turns to the palaces of cowrie and jade, and the towering view encompasses the terraces of elixir and herbs. This hall was completed in no time, and its grandeur is unmatched.

Furthermore, we honor the immortal officials of the Divine Music Abbey, the abbot and supervisor, whose immortal bearing is like the lotus pavilion, and whose demeanor is that of mist and rosy clouds. They tread the azure gates of the purple palace, and lead the grand music of the cloud gates. Their noble efforts in planning have made them the pillars of the mountains and forests.

We also honor the director of the Daoist Registry, the left master of the Dharma, whose refined scholarship governs the pivotal mechanisms of the Dao; whose breath commands wind and rain, and who holds the secret levers of power. Day by day, they receive abundant imperial favor, and devote their utmost to planning and effort.

Moreover, we honor the mountain-abiding supervisor, Master Li, whose jade carriage enhances the mountain’s splendor, and whose pearl-like virtue enriches the abyss. He explores the mysterious codes of the Dharma sea and assists the teaching’s seat in the pure capital. Together with the assembly of talented administrators and the many gentlemen who contributed gold, their fine reputations and noble aspirations have long shone in this enlightened age; their fragrant praise and virtuous renown resound together in the light of transformation.

This is the establishment of the teaching through the divine way, where wind and thunder shape its form. Now, the painted pillars and carved eaves gleam in the sky, dazzling the sun. How magnificent are the colorful columns and ornate doors, enveloped in mist and swirling wind! They unite the luminous clarity of the Azure Beginning and merge the true emptiness of the Great Red. The wondrous peaks and sacred ridges resemble the majestic postures of soaring dragons and phoenixes; the layered wheels and towering banners evoke the grandeur of clouds and mist. Fittingly, the myriad spirits gather in homage, and this is indeed a grand design for a thousand generations.

Thus, we raise the beam and respectfully offer this auspicious ode:

**East of the Beam**
Five clouds and auspicious mists swirl in the air,
The sun’s radiance illuminates the golden and silver palaces,
Mountains and peaks shine together in eternal glory.

**South of the Beam**
A thousand peaks and ten thousand ridges pile like indigo,
Rainbow banners and feathered standards...

Floating in the void below, a millet-grain hangs high as the northern face aligns with the Dipper.

**West of the Beam**
Jade groves and jasper grasses rise level with white clouds,
Sacred peaks array themselves in ordered ranks—
Green City stands revealed, its ten-thousand-kalpa cinnabar radiance linking to the Great Subtlety.

**North of the Beam**
Elephant Ridge rounds high in a single hue with heaven,
The Han Altar’s jade plan and myriad spirits’ reverence—
Fortune marks the imperial decree as all nations pay homage.

**Above the Beam**
Mist-borne chariots and rosy clouds, phoenix and crane in solemn array,
Jade Capital’s ethereal vastness, the Great Clarity’s domain—
The gods’ mysterious precincts are not without form.

**Below the Beam**
Cavernous scriptures and divine canons follow wondrous transformation,
Upon the Void Sovereign’s altar, moonlight shines bright—
The Four Numinous Ones surround the true immortal’s carriage.

We humbly pray that after the beam is raised, the imperial realm will grow ever vaster, and the mysterious teaching will shine with greater splendor. May the four quarters and eight wilds all be bathed in its nurturing grace; may the multitudes of people and all clans partake of its pure and tranquil winds. May the Dao’s domain know no bounds, and the lineage of immortals endure forever.

**Raising the Beam for the Founding Master’s Hall**

We reflect that when the blazing Han’s teaching flourished, Dragon-Tiger became the abode of divine immortals. Lord Liu’s lineage, marked by jade and scepter, became the model of noble heritage. Long has the celestial palace been revered; how could it resist the turning of kalpas’ dust? Human plans endure, and imperial power renews.

With reverence, we consider His Imperial Majesty, who opened the Nine-Five diagram and established the primal orthodoxy. With vast vision and towering wisdom, he set the imperial standard to build the center; with abundant virtue and great merit, he governed the celestial offices and bestowed the calendar. The grand foundations of Tang and Wu flourish anew; the flourishing achievements of Han and Tang are now extended. He cherishes the courtly traditions since Yu’s tribute and gathers the harmonies of Shun’s music to institute rites. As heir apparent, he fulfills the people’s hopes for a true and good ruler; as imperial prince, he secures the state and altars’ peace. Rightly do Hua and Yi alike rejoice in harmony, while the Dao’s domain receives exceptional favor. Plans and strategies expand daily, and the pillars of heaven stand revealed.

We reverently consider the Founding Master, the Orthodox Unity, Profound and Mysterious, Tranquil and Responsive, Manifest and Protective True Lord—whose Dao is revered in the mysterious court, whose teaching unfolds in the Pure Capital. With divine might like wind and thunder, he truly crowns the three mountains’ eminence; with cap, sash, sword, and pendants, he manifests the source and flow of an illustrious lineage. He accumulates blessings for the state and people, nurturing fragrance in descendants. Through the earthworm’s humble service, he receives the celestial court’s favor, suddenly magnifying the divine edifice’s majestic gaze. A thousand years’ grand design is now a single moment’s magnificent sight.

Moreover, we consider the worthy generals and ministers, the talented men of Min’s walls, and the great virtues of the four directions—all sharing an era’s glorious radiance. The Dao resides here, and the utmost spirit knows no bounds. The six directions follow heaven’s warp and earth’s weft; the five cities’ walls are attended by sun and clouds. Once, dragon-officials were driven to transport magnificent timber; soon, crane-borne decrees sought azure tiles. Wondrous wood was completed in the moon’s palace; southern gold arrived at the cloudy court. The Purple Capital’s twelve heavens transformed into Peng’s gates; the Jasper Capital’s thirty thousand households were moved from Fang and Ying. Truly, it resembles a conch-shell palace and cinnabar terrace, vast as the medicine steps and jasper halls. The isles of Feng and Lin, spring-warmed, revolve; the banners of phoenix and crane, their music resounding, descend from the Nine Clarities. Rainbow ranks and mist-borne carriages gleam like lightning, brushing the heavens. Without mountains and rivers’ majesty, how could the master and minister’s dignity be displayed? By the land’s elevated brightness, it fittingly crowns the admiration of humans and heavens. Thus, numinous spirits guard and escort, wind and thunder ever accompany the immortal capital; while pearls and jades shine brilliantly, the starry Han ascends to the imperial abode. Jade missives and gemmed scrolls—only Ge’s might compare; jade lotuses and golden stalks—perhaps Mao’s mound could rival. As we receive the forty-third transmission and rebuild for the fifteen-hundredth generation, though divine work is trustworthy, it is also the land’s numinous power that brings this to pass. Seizing the moment, it is completed in no time. With reverence for the six wefts, the twin beams are raised.

**East of the Beam**
Light divides the luminous peaks, the Dao like a dragon—
Spring returns to the calendar, the morning mound’s beauty,
All within the nurturing harmony of the long-lasting wind.

**West of the Beam**
The immortal terrace’s peaks rise level with clouds,
Jasper pools and jade trees stand beyond mist and rosy glow—
At times, celestial script descends in purple clay.

**South of the Beam**
Dust Lake soars high, rivaling Hua’s balance,
Cloud banners and mist standards array in emerald ranks—
The sun guards the White Jade Casket of eternal life.

**North of the Beam**
The Dao’s ancestor soars beyond all reckoning,
In crimson robes and fish-scale armor, solemn in layered heavens—
Since ancient times, the Han’s house has been the immortals’ abode.

**Above the Beam**
The ranked emperors dwell in a thousand-fathom vastness,
Numinous lords pay timely homage, roaming the Great Clarity—
The Jade Treasury’s pivotal mechanisms are passed down through generations.

**Below the Beam**
Tigers guard, dragons soar, phoenix carriages array,
Jade script shines bright amid the five clouds—
For kalpas without end, emptiness knows no day or night.

We humbly pray that after the beam is raised, the sagely lifespan will be as long as heaven, the imperial realm will flourish like a tripod, the heir’s glory will be magnified, and the world’s peace will be secured. May meritorious names rival Xiao and Cao’s; may household legacies emulate Yang and Guo’s. May the maple’s reach extend across rivers and seas, the mysterious wind flourish upon grand foundations; may virtue shine like coral and jade, the teaching’s lineage grow ever more prosperous in the imperial vessel. May the ancestral altar endure forever, and the Dao’s transformation know no bounds.

**Raising the Beam for the Three Gates**

We reflect that Dragon-Tiger’s famed mountain marks the blessed land of pure emptiness; Feng and Lin’s separate isles open the vast gate of the Dharma. After yesterday’s flames of separation, today’s reconstruction begins anew. The Dao’s model is made manifest, and divine transformation is made clear. We look up to the three realms’ exalted ones and the ten directions’ assembled sages. The Founding Master, the Orthodox Unity, Profound and Mysterious, Tranquil and Responsive, Manifest and Protective True Lord—who initiated the Orthodox Unity’s ancestral wind and unfolded the Mysterious Origin’s wondrous transformation. Possessing the strategic advantage of mountains standing and rivers flowing, he expanded the celestial warp and terrestrial weft’s guiding principles. Precious scriptures and jade texts extended the fifteen-hundred-year immortal lineage; pearl palaces and jade towers honored the twenty-four administrations’ divine merit. The gate channels the sun and moon’s passage; the door mirrors heaven and earth’s opening and closing. Its beauty is splendid, its majesty imposing.

Moreover, we consider the divine music’s immortal officials and the abbot’s guiding presence. Returning from the northern palace, he assumed the old seat of mist and rosy glow; resting on Eastern Mountain, he wore the rain and dew’s exceptional grace.

The illustrious title shines with glory, truly serving as the model for the gates of the Mysterious Dao.

Moreover, we consider the revered master who oversees the mountain’s affairs: his jade-like essence and golden voice ascend to pay homage to the dragon’s resplendent play; his flawless pearl and unblemished jade dignify the crane’s hall of governance. In assisting the great accomplishment, his plans and strategies endure forever.

Moreover, we consider the master of the Daoist Register who oversees the left division: his literary grace and historic purity, his majestic bearing like wind and thunder. Honored with the weight of golden seals, favored with the esteem of the precious pavilion, he especially aids the mountain forests and completes the halls and beams.

As for the divine treasures’ offices and the skilled artisans’ talents, their grand achievements and mighty deeds fittingly illuminate the Mysterious Pivot; their splendid promotions and fine reputations together ascend to the pure selection.

All things possess form and thus possess norms; the divine, being formless, is boundless. Resplendent are the carved pillars of the ornate halls, arrayed amidst clouds and mist. Suddenly, the painted walls encircle with inscriptions, lightning flashes across the sky. Jade chimes harmonize with the rainbow banners’ procession; the towered paths descend spirits with feathered regalia. Gem-like peaks and jade trees display the bearing of soaring dragons and leaping leopards; cloud pendants and rosy banners dignify the steps of cranes and phoenixes in attendance. This is the guard of a hundred spirits, the gaze and reliance of ten thousand families.

Swiftly, twin rainbows rise, uniquely arraying the six celestial wefts.

**To the East of the Beam:**
The sun’s radiance dawns, crimson upon the sea’s mounds; the sacred altar stands solemn, guarded by wind and thunder. Amidst the purple haze, the pass floats in the glow of dawn.

**To the South of the Beam:**
The cinnabar carriage and crimson regalia descend upon phoenix glue; the bright court bestows distant celestial incense, the imperial palace’s edicts gleam upon the jeweled seals.

**To the West of the Beam:**
The jade grove’s crisp air suffuses the misty cliffs; the jasper altar’s night candles burn with crimson light, the golden well’s divine spring murmurs in the Purple Tenuity.

**Below the Beam:**
Feathered pendants and morning jades align in procession; the Mysterious Wind stirs the four seas, awakening the people’s gaze. The Five Blessings are sung in harmony with the sagely transformation.

We humbly pray that after the beam’s raising, the imperial realm will expand boundlessly, the Dao’s virtue like spring’s radiance. A hundred blessings and a thousand auspices will equally bear the refining grace; the Five Winds and Ten Rains will all reside within nurturing embrace. The Dao’s transformation will grandly manifest, the true wind ever more vibrant.

*Xianquan Ji*, Scroll Six concludes
*Xianquan Ji*, Scroll Seven begins

**A General Explication on the Transmission of the Three Primes**
*Composed by Celestial Master Zhang Yu Chu of Mount Longhu, the Perfected of Non-Action*

The Great Void is profound and boundless, its subtle pattern obscure and minute—so ultimate it defies speech, so wondrous it eludes thought. Before sound or scent, form or name, the vast Brahman of the Qi River stretched empty and lightless. In that time, scripture had not yet arisen; it was inconceivable, immeasurable.

When the Crimson Clarity unfolded its chart, heaven and earth were born, and the ten thousand existences took form. A hundred thousand layers of Dao-darkness coalesced into cloud-script, issuing forth as numinous texts. Only then did the myriad patterns unfold, the Five Canons scatter forth, preserving and regulating the kalpas, enduring with heaven itself. The transmission among true sages remains one in principle.

From the Primordial Beginning’s discourse on the scriptures in the suspended millet-pearl radiance, the assembled perfected oversaw the conferral upon the Jade Dawn Dao Lord, and the Great Pattern first unfurled. After the Kaihuang era, the Great Vehicle of the Numinous Treasure was again transmitted, along with the *Purple Tenuity’s Flying Celestial Ten Divisions* and the *Primordial Beginning’s Cavernous Mystery Numinous Treasure Red Writ Jade Chapters*, the *Chaotic Vastness Primal Nothingness Numinous Text*. The Primordial Beginning refined it in the Cavern Yang’s Hall, smelted it in the Flowing Fire’s Court—thus the Primordial Beginning Numinous Treasure’s mysterious root, the Cavernous Void’s spontaneous true writ, which generates heaven and establishes the pole, enlightens the divine luminaries, deploys its numinous might to pacify the Five Peaks, and brings peace to the realm and well-being to the people.

Therefore, the Most High expounded the Jade Bureau, and the numinous writ spread forth. Then our Han Ancestor, the Celestial Master, descended in response to the transformation. In the first year of the Shanghuang era, on the fifteenth day of the first month, the Most High Lord of the Limitless Dao inscribed the Eight Upper Transformations. In the first year of the Limitless era, on the fifteenth day of the seventh month, he inscribed the Eight Middle Transformations. In the second year of the Limitless era, on the fifteenth day of the tenth month, he inscribed the Eight Lower Transformations.

In the second year of Han’an, on the fifteenth night of the first month, he was moved by the Golden Watchtower’s Later Sage Primordial Dao Lord, who descended upon Mount Heming in Western Shu. There, he conferred the *Secret Register of the Orthodox Unity Alliance威 Capital for Cultivating Perfection and Prolonging Life, with Flying Transformation*, along with the *Elbow-Behind Scripture and Oral Instructions*. In the seventh month of that year, he established the Twenty Western Treaties and transmitted them to his successor. Then, on the fifteenth day of the tenth month, he founded the Four Treaties to correspond with the Twenty-Eight Constellations. Thus, the Treaties encompass the Twenty-Four Qi, and each Qi governs Twenty-Four Offices. There are Twenty-Four Male and Female Officials, and Twenty-Four Male and Female Offices. Upon receiving their appointments, they follow the statutes and regulations to govern households and transform the people.

Those who delight in the Dao and rejoice in the law, whose hearts are single-minded and wills unwavering, are delivered from calamity and granted extended years. They subdue the perverse and return to orthodoxy, dispel harm and expel demons, rescue the living and deliver the dead. In the highest degree, they may ascend in spirit and tread upon radiance, transcend ranks and attain perfection, ensuring that the teaching of the Three-Five endures for endless kalpas, and the true wind of Orthodox Unity flows without cease.

Thus, those who receive the transmission face the deities of the Treaties and deliverance, standing before the altar to divide the registers, thereby manifesting the gravity of the covenant. The Dao Lord once declared: “When I descended to the Shu capital, the Twenty-Four Treaties were all prisons of the Twenty-Eight Constellations, known as the Bureaus of the Dark Registers of Yin Radiance. There, I opened the Jade Dawn Palace of the Purple Yang Southern Court and conferred the *Secret Register of the Orthodox Unity Alliance威 Capital*. From it, I obtained the Way of traversing the Celestial Stem and treading the Dipper, the essentials of the Three Steps and Nine Traces.”

He once told the Ancestral Master Perfected Lord: “The Dao of Orthodox Unity was born from the primordial chaos, before the dark and yellow had taken shape, when purity and simplicity still prevailed. As the Great Simplicity began to scatter and the frivolous wind daily encroached, I feared the Dao-folk would be led astray by the perverse, the primordial qi would become mixed and confused, ghosts and demons would entangle them, calamities would arise wantonly, and they would fail to attain the true Dao, their heavenly years cut short by harm. Thus, I descended the Alliance威 tally to covenant against external perversity and rectify the internal primordial darkness—hence the name Orthodox Unity. Those who invoke it perceive the Dao of the undivided source. Therefore, this method is the gateway to all methods, encompassing the Upper Clarity’s Ten Transformations and Nine Changes, the Great Red’s *Hidden Writ of the Three-Nine Plain Words*.”

The Ancestral Master Perfected Lord also once instructed Perfected Wang: “The primordial darkness of the Chaotic Origin is fundamentally one. One generates two, two generates three—these are called the Three Primes. Three generates four, four generates five—these are the Five Phases. These Three Primes and Five Darknesses weave heaven and earth, transform the myriad things. Thus, the method of Orthodox Unity is born from the primordial darkness, dynamically transforming through the Five Phases—hence the name Three-Five Method. Those who uphold it align with the Three Primes of the Imperial Lords, stabilize the Five Phases, guard the principles of sun and moon, rectify the luminous and obscure, follow the sequence of thunder and lightning. There is no reckless movement in wind and clouds; the ten thousand things flourish in moisture. The realm knows no toil of warfare, the people suffer no afflictions of pestilence. Such is the great resonance of upholding the Orthodox Unity method.”

The Perfected Lord first dwelled in Songyang, then traversed the famous mountains east of the river, following the great gorges. Entering Shu, he subdued demons and vanquished specters, dividing the dark prisons into Twenty-Four Courts of Blessing and demoting the demon marshals to Twenty-Four Yin Officials. There, he encountered the Primordial Dao Lord, who again conferred upon him the *Orthodox Unity Alliance威 Way*, the *Three-Eight Flying Immortality and Life-Prolonging Arts*, and invested him as the Supreme Mystery Capital Orthodox Unity Perfected, assuming the Later Sage’s position of the Primordial, becoming the Great Dharma Master of the Mysterious Center. He was enfeoffed as the Lord of the Supreme Mystery Capital Orthodox Unity Pacification Darkness Palace.

Upon pacifying the demonic hordes of the Six Heavens and completing his cultivation, the decree of the Three Heavens descended, and he ascended in broad daylight, taking his place among the Nine Clarities. Thus, the transmission of the Twenty-Four Rank Secret Registers all subdue the perverse and return to orthodoxy, greatly flourishing the numinous transformation to bless the myriad people. They descend the darkness of the Twenty-Eight Constellations, cultivate the governance of the Twenty-Four Darknesses, wear the talismanic cords and seals, command the generals and officials of the Treaties and Systems. When merit is complete and virtue perfected, the Three Officials endorse and recommend them. Their names are inscribed in jade, they undergo corpse liberation and transformation, ascend to the rank of Perfected, and their seven generations of ancestors ascend to the Hall of Blessing. Hence, the transmission of the Three Caverns and Four Supplements’ scriptures and registers expands and propagates the secret and wondrous, universally delivering the boundless.

The above serves to safeguard and secure the nation’s destiny, ensuring it endures with Heaven, while below it bestows blessings upon the living and the deceased, so that all under Heaven rejoice. Thus, within the Purple Yang Inner Palace, the *Jade Dawn Orthodox Unity* secret canon unfolds and expounds the profound and subtle—rightly so.

To this day, after forty-three transmissions, it has received the sacred favor and flowed forth from the ancestral altar. Now, on this auspicious festival of the Upper Prime, the day when the Heavenly Officials review the records, the chief disciple of the central altar, [Name], presents golden offerings in devotion, beseeching the descent of profound grace. Practitioners from the ten directions, adorned with talismans, gather at the ancestral altar. Thus, the high companions of the Dharma ocean, the pure assembly of the lecture hall, purify body and mind, desiring to hear the supreme Dao.

As the scriptures say: “From the void and spontaneity the Dao arises; the True One is undivided, its essence serene. Round and luminous, self-sufficient, it does not fall into views, far removed from dust and defilement. Learning is no-learning, cultivation is no-cultivation—within this, all is clearly understood. Neither departing nor abiding, neither death nor birth—this is true awakening.” How could this not be deeply and brilliantly evident?

Cultivated inwardly, it is the Dao of the Golden Elixir’s return to the Three and Five; applied outwardly, it is the wondrous efficacy of the *Numinous Treasure’s* Ten Revolutions of the True One. Expounded, it becomes the texts of the *Purple Pivot* and *Flying Sanskrit*, the records of the *Cinnabar Scripts* and *Numinous Charts*. Universally delivering heaven and humanity, its merit is boundless. Thus, the transmission of the Supreme’s various scriptures and registers, originating from this, fully encompasses the Dao of responsive transformation.

For the pivot of creation can transform our people—like Heaven descending and Earth ascending, encircled by sun and moon, activated by thunder and lightning. Its mechanism operates without speech, yet benefits the parched and gives life. Thus, those endowed with humanity are neither enhanced by wisdom nor diminished by folly; it lies in turning inward to seek the inherent goodness, moment by moment returning to the real, pure and undivided. Only then, embracing the mysterious and guarding the One, restoring simplicity and preserving the true, are the Dao of fulfilling one’s nature and destiny fully realized.

Therefore, the myriad things share a single root, moving in harmony with Heaven and Earth without conflict. The Dao’s foundation lies in emptiness, tranquility, stillness, and non-action. Applied to family and state, extended to heaven and humanity, there is no realm where it does not prevail. Its responses to the two realms (spiritual and mundane) all arise from the true texts and numinous talismans, which avert calamity and bring forth auspiciousness—truly, there is a reason for this.

Thus, its benefits extend beyond merely blessing the living and the dead. Bathed in the Supreme’s nurturing grace, its boundlessness is assured. Tonight, ascending this Dharma seat, the High Perfected of the Celestial Court bear witness to the covenant. The six realms of existence and the four sagely ranks form the audience. Briefly expounding these teachings, may profound awakening be attained.

All good and faithful people, all sentient beings, may you equally ascend to benevolence and longevity. May none remain bound in the unseen, but together reach the shore of the Dao. Having stood long, take care.

*Universal Refining and Deliverance: A General Exhortation*

We have heard that the wondrous precepts of the *Cavern of Perfection* and the jade texts of the *Numinous Treasure* uphold the nation’s destiny for ten thousand years and deliver the suffering souls from the vast kalpas. Their prohibitions are most solemn, their divine power beyond thought. They universally deliver the departed spirits who, having long transgressed the true Dao, willingly endure cycles of retribution. First, the sacred milk of the Dharma must be widely proclaimed to illuminate their true nature, that they may swiftly awaken and early depart the dark paths.

Originally, before the beginning of the Limitless, prior to the Great Origin, there were no signs, no omens. Then the Great Simplicity first dispersed, yin and yang first divided, Heaven was established and the pole set, the myriad things were born and nurtured, the Three Powers stood together, and humanity dwelt among them. Yang transformed and yin united, the Five Phases congealed, the Two Qi circulated. All things, born together with Heaven and Earth, equally received the One Qi and took form. With form came endowed nature—this is the flowing of Heaven’s mandate.

When the Three Luminaries shine together, the Five Peaks stand in majesty, the wonders of thunder and the teachings of rain and dew—nothing, from the vast to the minute, lacks the fullness of innate knowledge. There is no single thing that does not possess this Supreme Ultimate. The divine Dao establishes teachings to deliver the world and transform humanity—only this.

Thus it is said: “The Dao of Heaven and Earth is undivided in its manifestation.” In Confucius and Mencius, it is called benevolence and righteousness; in Śākyamuni, perfect enlightenment; in Zhuangzi and Liezi, emptiness and non-being; in Xunzi and Yangzi, the balance of power; in Ban Gu and Sima Qian, literary expression. Flowing into the hundred crafts and thousand arts, it does not depart from the inch of the heart. Though paths differ, the return is one—myriad things share a single root.

Yet Heaven and Earth and all existence are bound to form and qi, confined to the cycles of arising and ceasing, flourishing and withering, formation and decay. Human life, with the stirring of consciousness, is assailed day and night by incessant disturbance, never a moment’s rest. Ears hear, eyes see, mouth tastes, heart thinks—all are obscured by desire, entangled by emotion, seized by circumstances, lured by objects.

For nature flows into emotion, emotion blazes into thought, thought accumulates into anxiety, anxiety endures into consciousness. Thus, within the seven apertures, the six desires and five aggregates, the three poisons—all greed, anger, hatred, love, joy, resentment, conflict, and opposition—entangle and bind, growing ever deeper and more fixed. One sinks into the dust of the root-qi’s single boat, bound by clinging thoughts, even to the point of owing karmic debts through love and desire, forming enmity. Mistaking strangers for kin, enmity and kinship intertwine, mutually avenging. Thus, the body’s senses arise, and circumstances follow the mind’s birth.

All adverse and favorable, good and evil circumstances, with the slightest movement, become obstacles. With form comes the sprouting of a single thought, pursuing delusion and illusion. For a hundred thousand kalpas, the turning never ceases—rising in the east, setting in the west, emerging and submerging. Even wood and stone, without memory, are constantly moved, all due to a single thought’s deviation. Thus, a thousand lifetimes of suffering arise, one’s spirit sinking, drifting, scattered, and confused, with no end in sight.

At first, the skandhas of form, sensation, perception, mental formations, and consciousness seem real, giving rise to the retributions of heaven and hell. Yet they know not that earth, water, fire, wind, sound, and form are all empty flowers.

Delusion.

Since the vast kalpas of primordial chaos, through the long night of the Nine Dark Realms, suffering and affliction have been boundless. Thus, the Great Unity above, possessing the virtue of cherishing life, opened the gate of expedient means, arising in great compassion to universally guide all beings, enabling them to abandon delusion and return to truth, equally attaining the supreme fruit of the Dao, gaining immeasurable blessings, and forever emerging from deep delusion.

Carefully examined: The Primordial Celestial Unity, the Most High, suspended a precious pearl in the Azure Heaven of Beginnings, summoning the thousand perfected ones to expound the precepts of the Mysterious and Yellow qi. All entering into formation, abiding, decay, and destruction are created by the mind and veiled by wind, the four great elements merely a temporary convergence. All that possesses form is but illusion; only the formless is perfectly luminous, eternally unfolding its wondrous teachings. These were transmitted to the Jade Emperor, the Numinous Treasure Dao Lord, and thus the Three Grades of the Numinous Treasure Dao emerged.

Next, they were passed to the Five Elder Thearchs and the Perfected One of Wondrous Conduct. King Zhen of Jade Purity opened the Vermilion Numinous Fire Mansion, issuing the talismanic decree to shatter hell. The Great Emperor of Azure Splendor opened the Left Mansion of Azure Splendor, issuing the Nine Dragons Talismanic Decree. The Venerable Lord Han opened the Vermilion Spring Mansion of Spring, issuing the Talismanic Decree to Deliver Souls from Darkness. The Three Assisting Perfected Ones opened the Yellow Register Court, issuing the Yellow Register Perfected Talismans. Thus, the Three Masters of Antiquity, through the *Millet and Pearl Scripture*, expounded the arcane texts of refinement and deliverance, liberating the souls of the dead and extending blessings to the myriad kinds.

The Numinous Treasure Celestial Worthy transmitted these to the Grand Pure Dao and Virtue Celestial Worthy, who in turn passed them to the Great Recluse, the Master of Myriad Things, who entrusted them to the *Flying Celestial Jade Scripts of the Ten Divisions*, thereby unfolding their subtleties in an unbroken lineage. By the Han dynasty, our ancestral Celestial Master received the transmission of the Orthodox Unity, its texts still flourishing.

At the beginning of the Han, the *Chaotic Red Writ of Brahmā’s Net*, inscribed by the Heavenly Perfected Sovereign, consisted entirely of cavernous numinous talismans. Above, they safeguard the turning of the kalpas and eliminate the three disasters; below, they refine the souls of the dead and deliver the living. Universally proclaimed to the boundless divine realms, the Northern Metropolis of the Yellow Springs, they swiftly erase the ledgers of sin, extinguishing the roots of evil. Then, demon kings offer protection, earth officials escort the departed, and souls are delivered from the earthly gates to ascend as perfected beings.

Yet, as the world declines and customs grow shallow, the arcane texts and profound canons remain hidden in the celestial treasuries, transmitted but once every forty thousand kalpas—only to those who have planted numinous roots in past lives. How could their boundless wonders be carelessly revealed? Their mysteries are of the utmost gravity; how could the negligent or arrogant fathom their subtleties?

Their wonder lies in delivering people. The merit of delivering others is often heard from the immortal masters: "The Numinous Treasure is the Golden Elixir’s treasure." If metal and wood remain separate, water and fire estranged, how can nature and life merge, returning to the origin and restoring the root? One must establish the cauldron and vessel of heaven and earth, refine the medicinal substances of Kan and Li, capture the leaping hare, unite the black dragon and tiger, gather the primordial True Unity’s qi as the foundation, and take the mechanism of yin-yang’s movement as the model. In motion, it arises from the Nine Yangs; in stillness, it follows the sixty-four hexagrams as the fire phases of the celestial cycle. The circulation adheres to the three yin and six yang, yet the Numinous Treasure’s completeness lies in the Numinous Treasure.

The Golden Elixir is the Numinous Treasure; the four lines of the hexagram serve as the tally for ascent and descent. The wonder of inversion, the mechanism of reversal—extracting mercury from cinnabar—though myriad sages may ponder, none can fully grasp it! Thus, even the slightest deviation cannot be tolerated; the wonder lies in the Dao of the Three and Five returning to One. Open the crescent moon, move the celestial root, circulate along the ecliptic through the celestial cycle. Discern the embryonic spirit’s transformation in the dark chamber, the mysterious merging into form, refining and returning to truth.

Of old, the Supreme Primordial Sovereign attained the Dao of the Nine-Five, and the Lords of the Five Thunders attained the Dao of the Three-One, differing not from this. For the *River Chart* and *Luo Writing* reveal the root of heaven and earth’s generation. As for the Numinous Treasure: spirit congeals into numinosity, qi gathers into treasure. One must gather the qi of the primordial chaos and profound darkness, refine the essence of the sun’s soul and moon’s spirit, traverse the Southern Dipper, cross the Eastern Well, activate the true fire of utmost yang, and descend the yellow essence of great yin. Thus, Kan’s lunar essence and Li’s solar radiance merge, the five qi circulate through the celestial cycle, form arising from the formless, ascending directly to the Vermilion Numinous Realm.

This is the universal deliverance: the dead refined, the living delivered, souls crossing the Vermilion Numinous Realm to undergo refinement and rebirth. It is the emptiness of the One symbolizing the Supreme Ultimate, returning to non-being. Thus, the perfected cultivate it to refine themselves and extend it to deliver others. It is indeed the true yang of heaven and earth, transmuting yin spirits, ceaselessly ascending and advancing.

Know then that the Numinous Treasure is another name for the Golden Elixir. You, suffering souls, have endured kalpas of torment. Now, through the merit of the assembly leader [Name], the supreme great fast is established, a celebration of a thousand lives, allowing you to bathe in the Dao’s compassion and be instantly delivered. Having heard these wondrous teachings, they will forever become the seed of sagehood within you.

Your dharma-body of self-nature is originally without defilement, without birth or death. Yet, deluded by false illusions, you remain without awakening. The scripture states: "The beings of the three realms are originally without transmigration; the True Unity’s qi is originally without birth or death. The苦 sea is boundless; turn your head, and the shore is near." Thus it is said: "When understood, karmic obstacles are fundamentally empty; when not understood, one must repay past debts."

If the wise hear or see evil, they must know and awaken to it, sweeping it away. The foolish, lacking all aspiration, blindly wander in darkness and must urgently awaken. Those in wealth and nobility are entangled in every thought; those in poverty and lowliness cling to every thought. Having created these karmic causes, how can they escape the cycle of rebirth?

Therefore, the masters of former times ceased all activity, like cold ashes or dead embers, withered wood or stubborn stone. Only by stilling this single thought can one illuminate all delusions, not clinging to a single speck of dust.

Moreover, there is no beginning to coming, no end to going—birth is fundamentally non-birth, death fundamentally non-death. The wondrous existence of the single spirit endures eternally in an instant.

This arises from love as its root and accumulated thoughts as its karma, giving rise to manifold rebirths and manifold karmic retributions. Through a thousand lives they revolve, through ten thousand kalpas they suffer, ceaselessly turning without self-awareness. Disciples of the four assemblies, receiving the deliverance of departed spirits: I speak without tongue, you listen without mind. In that realm beyond speech and hearing, awaken fiercely—ultimately transcending all conditions, surpassing all illusions—then the three karmas and six senses will be instantly purified. Turning back, you suddenly realize that all past entanglements of suffering and joy are fundamentally unattainable. In this direct recognition, you realize that originally there was no birth, and now there is no death. Even the search for entanglements yields nothing—how much less do all deluded thoughts of existence and non-existence remain?

Do not assume this was possessed before birth and lost after death. Whether from kalpa to kalpa, abandoning one body to enter another, you remain indestructible. It is only your own delusion. If you clearly awaken to your inherent nature and contemplate your wondrously pure, luminous mind—radiant and numinous—it transcends speech and silence, movement and stillness, and clings neither to existence nor to boundaries. Like a mirror polished of all grime, the moon appears in the still water. The emptiness that is not empty is true emptiness; the thought that is without thought is right thought. In every movement, thorough illumination; in every thought, perfect interpenetration—truly, "a thousand rivers hold water, a thousand rivers hold the moon; ten thousand miles without clouds, ten thousand miles of sky."

If you do not shatter these barriers, you will forever remain in the old rut. You must directly perceive and bear witness—do not let this moment slip by. A hundred thousand Dharma gates, infinite wondrous meanings—all converge in a single moment of awakening. From this, when not a single thought arises, all conditions become still. Even the sins as numerous as grains of sand vanish, and only this original face remains—the true immortal and Dao ancestor. How then could there be hells or evil destinies, or the ceaseless suffering of rebirth?

When this ultimate realization is attained, all illusions are empty, and the One Reality alone manifests. The vast emptiness is without form—this is your true nature. Having heard this Dharma sound, the assembly suddenly awakens, recognizing their original true nature. They turn from the cycle of rebirth and never regress. Constantly guarding and upholding this, they become vast and perfectly luminous, utterly free from obstruction. Gazing upon all forms, what remains? Thus they transcend the Three Realms and wander freely in the Upper Clarity.

Yet for those souls still mired in the lower realms who have not fully realized the true and constant, it is fitting to transmit the precepts to prevent their fall. With reverence, the Nine Wondrous Precepts are proclaimed one by one. First, take refuge in the Three Treasures, that they may have a foundation. Let the departed souls of the netherworld be instructed, and let each uphold them.

**Transmission of the Dharma, General Exposition**

In the beginning of the Great Ultimate, the primordial chaos first divided, and from this arose the separation of yin and yang. Heaven and earth took their places, and the ten thousand things were nurtured. The Five Phases emerged, and the myriad transformations were born—thus, generation upon generation, transformation upon transformation, without end.

The Five Phases are but yin and yang; yin and yang are but the Great Ultimate. By the flowing movement of Heaven’s mandate, it bestows upon the ten thousand things their nature. When nature sprouts, principle is inherent within; when principle manifests, emotions appear without—all governed by the life and death of yin and yang, the ascent and descent of the Five Phases. Thus, water and fire clash, thunder and lightning strike, hardness and softness grind, the eight trigrams interact. Stirred by thunder and lightning, moistened by wind and rain, the workings of yin and yang are overseen by the divine ruler.

The waxing and waning of the ten thousand things are governed by the Emperor. Yet movement and stillness have no origin, yin and yang no beginning. In the human heart, this ruler is called the Emperor; its wondrous functioning is called spirits and gods. The vastness of heaven and earth is bound to yin and yang—how could it lack a ruler? This is what is meant by the Emperor.

The ancestral lineage of our Dao traces back to the Primordial Heavenly King, who, after the Opening of the Imperial Era, transmitted the Great Vehicle of the Numinous Treasure, the *Scriptures of the Ten Departments of the Purple Tenuity Flying Heaven*, to the Jade Clarity Great Dao Lord and the Nine Divine Empyreans of the Divine Empyrean. Later, descending upon Mount Emei, he bestowed upon the Heavenly Perfected Sovereign the methods of refinement and deliverance. At the beginning of the Dragon Han kalpa, the Nine Yangs of spontaneous qi emerged. The Primordial Beginning commanded the Heavenly Perfected Sovereign to take up the brush and compose the text, which was concealed in the Cavern of Yang. When the Vermilion Numinous Fire Treasury was opened, the scriptures for reviving the dead and restoring life were entrusted to him—thus, the *Scriptures of Millet Pearls* unfolded into the texts of refinement and deliverance.

During the Dragon Han kalpa, the Dao Lord was also bestowed with the wondrous and mysterious Dao of Pure Tenuity, while the Elder Lord received the inner methods of the Primordial Response. Thus, the Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy transmitted the *Perfect Formula of Pure Tenuity and Mysterious Penetration* to the Heavenly Emperor of Wondrous Transformation, and the Most High transmitted it to him. Our ancestral Heavenly Master of the Han orally transmitted this as the Orthodox Lineage of Pure Tenuity. Later, in the Yuan dynasty, it was presented to the Imperial Consort Yuan, the Radiant Ancestral Mother, and thus unified as the *Pure Tenuity, Numinous Treasure, Dao Virtue, Orthodox Unity*.

The Perfected Xu of the Great Ultimate cultivated the Dao and attained realization. By the command of the Most High, he was entrusted with the *Ten Wondrous Scriptures of the Numinous Treasure*. The Perfected Xu transmitted them to the Three Assistant Perfected Ones, under whose charge all matters of deliverance were placed. The Three Assistant Perfected Ones transmitted them to the Left Palace Immortal Duke of the Great Ultimate, from whom the lineage of the Numinous Treasure flourished and spread. Those who propagated its teachings—such as Du, Lu, Ning, and Zhang—achieved the greatest prominence. Among those who transmitted it to later generations, none were more eminent than the two patriarchs, Lin and Bai. This is called the *Emergence of the Cavern Real, Deliverance of Humanity*, provisionally named the *Primordial Beginning*; the *Succession of the Cavern Mystery*, alternatively called the *Numinous Treasure*; and the *Elaboration of the Cavern Spirit*, named the *Dao Virtue*. Though these three differ in name, in reality they are one.

Formerly, the Primordial Beginning Heavenly Worthy commanded the Perfected King of Jade Clarity to open the Vermilion Numinous Fire Treasury, the Great Emperor of Azure Radiance to open the Left Treasury of Azure Radiance, and the Venerable Lord Han to open the Right Treasury of the Vermilion Numinous. The Three Assistant Perfected Ones opened the Yellow Register Court and produced the talismans of the *Jade Clarity, Earth-Prison Breaking*, and the texts of the *Three Writs and Five Talismans*. In all practices of refinement and deliverance, when proclamations are issued to the netherworld gates, none fail to awaken.

The above is called the *Divine Empyrean*, descending from the *Limpid Tenuity*; all these are its texts. Thus, the Supreme Divine Empyrean Jade Clarity Perfected King, the Great Emperor of Longevity, exclusively governs the Nine Empyreans and the Thirty-Six Heavens’ Worthies. The Thirty-Six Heavens’ Worthies are solely commanded by the Great Emperor, who oversees the primordial configurations and holds dominion over yin and yang. Therefore, the administration of thunder and lightning is entirely subject to him.

Formerly, the Supreme Primordial Sovereign attained the Way of the Nine and Five. The Scripture states: "One who attains the Way of the Nine and Five becomes the Emperor of Thunder." The Five Thunder Lords thus obtained the Way of the Three-in-One Thunder. Three is the ancestral number of the East, and One is the generative number of the North.

The Immortal Master said: "The Supreme Unity Primordial Sovereign revealed the utmost truth, manifesting the Three and Five to deliver ordinary beings." In the *Numinous Treasure* teachings, the vastness of Heaven and Earth, the solar essence and lunar spirit, ceaselessly ascend and descend in the interplay of yin and yang. The method by which the dead are refined and the living delivered lies in using one’s yang spirit to refine their yin souls, thereafter harmonizing yin and yang to return to the Supreme Ultimate, merging nature and destiny to revert to the primordial origin. Thus it is said: "Congeal the spirit into numinosity, gather the qi into treasure." Spirit is nature; qi is destiny. For the Empty Cavern descends numinosity, the Great Void generates spirit, and the Golden Womb of the Void is the true within the true. Therefore, the spirit and qi are concealed within the Three Fields and Five Viscera, drawing from the celestial *Ren* and *Hao* constellations. By repeatedly tasting the sweet dew, one gathers emotions to restore nature, gathers nature to return to the root. With water and fire in mutual completion, the Way of nature and destiny is perfected.

Thus, the Dao draws upon the sun and moon within oneself, and the method follows the symbolic patterns of water and fire. With one’s own luminous yang nature, one awakens the yin spirit of the other. Borrowing the qi of the Nine Empyreans and Nine Yangs, one refines the substance and purges the form, riding the compassionate radiance of the Supreme Emperor to dispel the darkness of the Nine Springs. Only then are sins extinguished, the spirit made whole, and transformation into life achieved.

The Wood of the East Three combines with the Fire of the South Two—this is the dragon reborn in fire. The Metal of the West Four combines with the Water of the North One—this is the tiger reborn in water. Wu and Ji are the Earth of the central intent, the marvel of the Three and Five united as One. Precisely as it is said: "With Kan and Li in mutual completion, all returns to the center; only then does one realize the merit of the Three and Five."

As for talismans, registers, writs, and incantations, as well as the protocols and ritual texts, these are the graded ranks of the Dharma-gate, serving as the ladder and ferry for entering the Dao, the direct path to seeking the true. If one does not seek it within oneself, how can one use the merit of self-cultivation to deliver others? Upon investigation, the ultimate principle is never not one.

The Five Thunder Lords, having attained the Way of the Three-in-One, manifest the wondrous function of the Two Dipper Stars, which is the numerology of the *River Chart*. Thus, the Three-in-One is no different from the Nine and Five. For the pivot of yin and the mechanism of yang, thunder is good and lightning is fierce; yang thunder and yin lightning together govern the Seventy-Two Bureaus of Thunder. Thus, the *Kui* and *Ji* constellations serve as the offices for summoning thunder and dispatching lightning.

In thunder and lightning, the central qi of Heaven and Earth is obtained. Jia and Geng are the commands of thunder and lightning, which is the function of the Nine and Five. Ren is the configuration of thunder, Bing is the convergence of thunder, and Zi is the origin of thunder. Thus, Zi is the first configuration of thunder, Mao is the gate of thunder, Wu and Gui are the offices of thunder-fire. When combined with the cyclical transformations of *Yanlü*, *Shunshen*, and *Gengshen*, all derive from the marvel of the Nine and Five. Through the Fire Master Wang the Perfected and the Perfected King of the Awaited Palace, the transmission of the Thunder Mother was fully revealed.

Humans, endowed with a single numinous spirit, together with Heaven and Earth form the Three Powers. The transformations of a single body’s yin and yang proceed in unison with Heaven and Earth without deviation. Alas! A single point of numinous clarity illumines Heaven and Earth; from ancient times to the present, none have recognized it. The Confucians call it "empty numinosity without obscuration," the Buddhists call it the "wondrously pure bright mind." Directly awakening to it, it is neither mind nor one; suddenly encountering it, it is neither Zen nor distant. The Scripture states: "Heaven issues its fierce mechanism, Heaven and Earth overturn; when Heaven and humanity are aroused, the old foundation is transformed." That which is called "humanity’s convergence with the Dao"—is this not the pivot of yin and the mechanism of yang?

When humans align with Heaven, harmony is achieved through the balance of yin and yang. Ghosts and spirits are the spontaneous functions of the Two Qi. By employing the mechanism of one’s own opening and closing to command them, this evokes and that responds. It begins with the Great Brahma’s primordial void, prior to the *Hun Dun* Red Script. Thereafter, the Five Classics unfold, and the myriad norms expand. The Five Scripts open and extend, universally establishing the numinous spirits. Thus, there is no scripture that does not deliver, no scripture that does not generate life.

In great matters, it can safeguard and stabilize the nation’s destiny, verify the Dao, and attain perfection. In small matters, it can protect oneself, pacify the household, aid others, and benefit all things. All are the comings and goings of a single qi, the mutual generation and restriction of the Five Phases. With one’s own primordial spirit from the infinite kalpas, one commands the spirits of the formless void. When spirit and qi unite, qi arrives and numinosity follows.

Thus, it is said: "Do not depart from the present moment’s constant clarity; seek to know the lord who cannot be seen." The establishment of the Dharma-gate of the Divine Empyrean for a single day is like the palm encompassing yin and yang, the executioner issuing commands, the messenger stirring the Milky Way, the thunder gate exchanging the movements of water and fire, the *Cavern Mystery* opening and closing the yin and yang, the Earth Lord strategizing the killing of spirits and deities, the arrow-killing techniques piercing the stellar luminaries. Below, there are the texts of Deng and Yue; above, there is the qi and the incantation. Thus, the divine methods of the moon and the divine techniques of the law are all derived from the wondrous functions within oneself, not merely from paper talismans and bodily postures. The method is the function of the Dao; the ritual is the vehicle of the method. The myriad spirits are but a single movement of the primordial Great Dao. When employing one’s own primordial spirit, filling it expands to pervade the Six Voids, gathering it contracts to not exceed a handful. How could the minute and the vast not be one? When one spirit moves, the myriad spirits follow.

The Immortal Master said: "Establish the Dao, and the method is also established; establish the method, and the Dao is also established." For embryo respiration, use the apertures; in every method, the heart must be able to penetrate the heart. Then one knows that gathering this is the true essential marvel of the method. Therefore, those who engage in cultivation must first investigate the wondrous function of the Mysterious Pass, the true source of water and fire, and the marvel of returning to the root and restoring destiny. Only then can one unite the myriad in the one, and the hundred considerations converge into one.

Should one fail to inwardly illuminate one’s nature—comprehending the celestial Dao and the thunderous heart-ground—how could one still the flesh to refine the golden elixir, or move like a thunderclap? Yet one must first temper conduct with resolute integrity and forge the path with diligent perseverance.

The Master said: "Within the real dwells the spirit; beyond sincerity, no method exists." Thus, preserving sincerity and nurturing qi form the essence, while penetrating the wondrous and seizing the mechanism serve as function. If one can embrace the origin and guard the one, steering darkness to congeal the spirit, the six senses dissolve into purity, the true singularity emerges, and I become the Thunderous Great Dharma King—what need remains for talismans, incantations, or secret formulas?

Though ascending to the Three Realms and transcending the myriad illusions may seem arduous, it is not so. The power to benefit and aid extends even to the mud-pill and mugwort, for both may lodge the handle of darkness and spirit. Thus, conversing and laughing amidst the wind and thunder are but trifling matters for me.

Yet the mysteries of transmission and reception, the secrets of talismanic script—all are inscribed in the golden statutes and jade regulations. Were they not transmitted through celestial descent, one by one, would there not arise the peril of beginning with zeal and ending in neglect? Therefore, the wondrous treasure of celestial truth is passed down through kalpas, with the descent of the celestial true origin governed by solemn vows and weighty covenants.

Now, the disciples beneath the altar, blessed across a thousand lives to ascend the immortal ranks, have received the lofty and profound transmission in accordance with the statutes. Thus, this numinous canon is expounded so that they may know the source from the stream, seek the root and discard the branches, and turn inward for an ever-abundant teacher.

Let none dare to treat these teachings with frivolous leakage or negligence, lest they violate the prohibitions. One must instead refine conduct with discipline, delve into the profound mysteries, and persist in cultivation without cease. As object and self are forgotten and spirit and illumination merge as one, shall one not tread the luminous path to transcendence and unite with the Great Void?

After all, before heaven and earth divided, where did the brush first touch? The myriad methods return to the one, but where does the one return? Let each strive diligently in receiving these teachings, without negligence.

**On the Restoration of the Yifa Guanzhou Monastery**

This monastery’s origins trace to the late Han, its foundations laid in the early Tang. By the flourishing Yuan, after centuries of decline, it had undergone repairs—yet the labor was vast. We now humbly appeal to the virtuous, entreating their aid in recompense, that this noble endeavor may be fulfilled.

It was the Celestial Master who descended as the Star of Literary Brilliance, cradled in auspicious clouds of lotus and kingfisher silk. The mountains, steeped in the numen of Liang and Chu, harbored dragon-tiger omens. The temple halls first rose in the Han, the palace courts flourished in the Tang. Through twelve hundred years, the twenty-four sacred precincts saw the Dao’s lineage grow ever more revered, the true wind ever more resplendent.

Alas! Storms and time have shaken its beams, leaving corridors to crumble and hemp to overgrow. Though the transmission of the teachings demands restoration, it is also the duty of true disciples to forge karmic ties. With brushstrokes that summon spring, may we witness Wang Chang’s peaches ripen anew; with vows made beneath the moon, may Zhao Lang’s tripod gleam once more. Let these halls of mother-of-pearl and pearl be no different from the cinnabar terraces and purple palaces. Let names be inscribed in the *Record of Longevity*, that blessings flow endlessly; let merits be recorded in the *Great Possession*, that auspicious order prevail. May the mystic wind endure forever, and the nation’s destiny know no bounds.

---

**Petition for the Restoration of Jing Tong Hermitage**

Jing Tong Hermitage was the cultivation ground of the Thirty-Third Celestial Master, the Perfected Lord Xu Jing. Born in the Xihe reign of the Song, he once gathered disciples atop Rounded Mountain, his merit and conduct resplendent. By the Chongning era, Emperor Huizong’s veneration of the Dao reached its zenith. Alongside the imperial attendants Wang Wenqing and Lin Lingsu, he enjoyed singular favor—his prayers and sacrifices to the cypress groves yielding wondrous signs. Soon after, the Song court fell, and the Perfected Lord, like his peers, attained liberation through seated transcendence. His surpassing deeds are fully chronicled in the records.

Yet the hermitage, built between the Song and Yuan, has suffered repeated devastation by war and fire, its reconstructions many. With the passage of years, its structures have inevitably decayed. Though this mountain’s restoration should take precedence, our strength is insufficient—we must rely on the collective karmic ties. Thus, we present this humble petition to the benevolent and generous, entreating their gold to accomplish this noble work. May the Perfected Lord’s numinous assembly, together with the multitude, bestow undying grace.

The Dao was honored when the Han court established the thirty celestial transmissions; the teachings unfolded when the Song dynasty penetrated the five thousand words’ mysteries. At the height of Emperor Huizong’s reverence, in concert with the illustrious attendants’ merits, he stationed brave generals in the palace courts and banished demonic dragons from the tides. Azure dragons and white tigers stood like emerald bamboo and jade parasols; red horses and vermilion sheep remained in the green annals and purple archives. Having adorned this hallowed ground, we must not forget the toil of its decay. To renew it, we must seek the aid of the wellsprings of generosity. As cranes return to the Liaohan Sea, may we gaze again upon the solitary flight toward the jade pavilion; as crows transform over the Sizhou Isles, may we rejoice in the towering splendor of the Jasper Terrace. Together, let us contribute to imperial favor and share in the numinous blessings.

*End of Volume Seven of the Jianquan Collection*
*Volume Eight of the Jianquan Collection*

**The "Ode to Tranquil Vastness" by Zhang Yuchu, the Non-Action Heavenly Master of Qishan**

When the Great Beginning’s profound vastness first stirred,
Myriad things drew sustenance from its generative power.
From the primal chaos, the first chisel struck,
And celestial patterns were arrayed as constancy’s script.
Rooted in movement and stillness, the first distinctions arose,
Alternating in marvelous pairs to form the Five Phases.
The sun’s charts and the earth’s records took this as their rule,
Establishing the Three Poles as the measure of all things.
Now bending, now rising in boundless expanse,
They vie in length through the work of creation.
When the Three and Five wondrously unite,
They coil like the pivot of a wheel, congealing within.
Swaddled in swaddling clothes, the infant stirs,
Resplendent yet elusive in its radiance.
Vast and empty, still and serene,
One seeks the dark pearl in the formless net.
A single grain of millet hangs in the void,
Majestic as clouds ascending and rainbows gleaming.
Embrace the compass within the hidden abyss!
Expand the floating vessel to harmonize the pure.
The heavens and earth revolve in cyclic gestation,
Harmonizing descent and ascent like the turning of a wheel.
Bathe in the Sun Valley and ascend to the imperial,
Soaring on mighty winds in boundless flight.
Urging forth the linked stalks of wisdom’s harvest,
I pay homage to the Radiant Lord in his dazzling splendor.
Sipping jade nectar and cassia wine,
I am veiled in the lush fragrance of jasper beams.
Then he bestowed upon me the words: "Vast and formless,
Transcend the tranquil vastness beyond the faintest echo."
Thus I cleanse this great defilement,
Returning the dark essence to its hidden store.
I mount the dim and frail carriage of the black-robed one,
Driving the six black steeds in their lush array.
Piercing the bright with the fullness of the dark,
I rein in my pace to move as a single breath.
How endless the cycles of beginning without end,
Swirling and eddying in ceaseless transformation!
I aspire to soar afar and attain it,
For only then may I savor the pure and true.
Pine and Paulownia, long-lived and proud,
What kinship have they with the common cypress?
Yet do they truly trust in fleeting life,
Lurking in the hardships of cliffs and valleys?
Their wills stand firm as ice and frost,
While the illusory world is but drifting dust.
How can splendor be called beauty?
Mired in filth, what room is there for debate?
Alas, my life is fraught with dullness,
My aspirations lingering in past fragrance.
The tangled threads of ancestral teachings,
Dampen my heart’s unspoken longing.
I yearn to delight in the great transformation,
Yet my balance beam is broken, my hidden thread concealed.
I cast aside indolence and lay down my staff,
Knocking at the vast gate to seek the ford.
I renounce the early cravings of mulberry and river,
For the great sound resounds like a distant echo.
Why treasure the gourd as a jewel,
When what use are the tripods of Shang?
I lament the discord of handle and socket,
As if my nature were estranged from its former fragrance.
Why still cling to the glow of fame,
Sighing in weariness for fleeting glory?
Who does not fortify their resolve?
Even the ancient sages prized steadfastness.
Yang Xiong guarded the mysterious,
Praising the root and cherishing the hidden gate.
Qu Yuan’s *Far Roaming*,
Also preserved its vital qi within.
Dredging the turbid to await the empty,
I rinse my mouth and hesitate.
Gazing afar at the distant corners of the world,
I should follow purity and shed my husk like a cicada.
Only Jia Yi’s lament for the roc,
Understood life and death as no cause for concern.
How much better to ride the limpid wind,
And reach the lightning’s strike without harm!
Cast off the excrescences of the self,
For what are things but fleeting bubbles?
Falling like morning stars in desolation,
Only a trace of light lingers and fades.
I grieve the dusty altar’s crudeness,
Wandering alone in sorrow and dismay.
I weave orchid sashes to leave behind,
Plucking ivy and dodder to untie my bonds.
I long to follow the fragrant steps,
Yet the lofty flight remains distant, and I am but a guest.
I gather dew upon chrysanthemum blossoms,
Moved by their purity, my form grows faint.
I equal self and other in a grain of rice,
Unconcerned by the desolation of the road.
I gaze up at the soaring phoenix,
Why begrudge its virtue’s radiance?
Fearful of the lame tortoise’s plodding,
I ride the glue-bound axle without reins.
I seek to knock at the Red Mound,
Yet who knows the mystery of wordless silence?

---

**The "Ode of Qishan"**

At the mountain’s peak,
None gaze upon the tortoise.
The trees of Mount Lu,
Unscarred by axe or adze.
In the mountain’s seclusion,
I dwell alone.
My will left behind,
The world sees only me.
When the imperial first arose,
Alas, where was I to witness it?

---

**The "Ode of the Woodcutter’s Return"**

I nest in the forest,
Who sees my cares?
Long have I yearned,
How dare I not follow?
Those who cherish the ancients,
Only guard their constancy.
I gather firewood,
Why let it be felled and harmed?
That ox has its lush pasture,
Why should I weigh its worth?
The world knows not my heart,
Why mourn my voice?

---

**The "Ode of the Orchid Sash"**

The orchid’s fragrance,
Its essence pure and clear.
I would wear it,
Who sees my thoughts?
Near or far,
Frost and snow cannot rend it.
On land near at hand,
Only brambles and thorns thrive.
I plant it in seclusion,
Grieving its hidden bloom.
Hidden, oh hidden,
Do not lift your fragrance,
Do not display your beauty.

---

**Imitating "The Spirit’s Release"**

The heavens’ edge is distant and hard to fathom,
Myriad things surge in endless flux.
The supreme principle melts into the great wheel,
One root branches into all creation.
The empty and numinous governs the subtle pivot,
The dark mechanism turns in nurturing poison.
Waxing and waning alternate in ceaseless play,
The mysterious and vast embraces all beings.
Luminous and clear, spanning the first beginning,
How can dust and defilement be bound?
Life and death are not two paths,
Short and long are but fleeting constraints.
The ancient immortals Pine and Paulownia,
Rode their steeds in carefree roaming.
I long to follow them,
Yet my lonely flight lags far behind,
Bound to the dusty altar.
How can I shed its filth,
Molding my form like a cicada’s molt?
Drowning in the foam, I yet lead my kind,
Gazing afar, I dwell in the six bones.
What use are excrescences,
When the hidden truth knows no bounds?
The abyss is clear, desireless,
Who says it is blind to joy or fear?
Day and night, I am ever buffeted,
Vast and empty beyond heaven and earth,
My breath like a flickering candle.
A thousand ages cast their lingering light,
The supreme spirit shines forever bright.

---

**Expressing My Feelings**

Alas, within the vault of heaven and earth,
A single breath swells in boundless might.
The cosmos fills the eight directions,
The empty and numinous abides in true awakening.
Ephemeral splendor gathers like moths,
Rebellious strife races like crocodiles.
Contending in clamor, trampling one another,
How can one attain the joy of Confucius and Yan Hui?
Frozen like ice, wary as treading frost,
Blazing like flames, startled by kindling.
Who grasps the balance of fate’s subtle workings?
I drift in tranquil detachment.
When sincerity and the Dao penetrate the first beginning,
How can the subtle and distant be fathomed?

The autumn sky stretches deep as a profound abyss,
The clearing moon gleams in the hidden ravine.
Through a thousand ages, what could compare?
In tranquil emptiness, I guard the serene void.

Cold and heat alternate in ceaseless succession,
Past and present ever shift and replace.
Vigorous movement turns without pause,
Round and square settle high and low.
Rain and dew—what is not instruction?
Wind and thunder complete the work of creation.
The supreme principle governs the dark mechanism,
Shaping and nurturing with measured art.

Great indeed is the embodiment of sincerity and clarity,
Cultivating and refining to weave purity.
To establish destiny is to build the foundation,
Following the model provides ample support.
Why let adornment stray from truth,
Or flaws and blights lack tempering and forging?
The banks of the Qi lie silent, their echoes faint,
The profound workings drift in sorrowful grace.

Confucius and Mozi walked distinct paths,
Mencius pursued a different noble labor.
Through perilous passes to Wei and Lu they ventured,
Yet who ultimately followed the kingly Way?
Chunyu’s will remained unbowed,
Gongsun Long claimed the firm and white.
The odes of Qi resounded with vigor,
